# Voynich Manuscript: Complete Interlinear Translation

**EVA Transcription with Croatian Reading - ALL FOLIOS**

**Total Folios:** 201

## The ZFD Three-Layer Key

| Layer | Position | Mapping |
|-------|----------|---------|
| Operators | Word-initial | q/qo -> ko, ch -> h, sh -> š |
| Gallows | Medial | k -> st, t -> tr, f -> pr, p -> pl |
| Suffixes | Word-final | y -> i, n -> n, r -> r, m -> m |

---

**Text:**

```
EVA: pcheol sheod qocpheeckhy shodol cthdaoto ch qeos sheey chcthso s
CRO: pheol šeod kocpllecstry šodol ctrrdaotro h koeos šei hctrrso s
```
```
EVA: dsheor cthey qokeey oteey ykeeodain sorary daiin daiin deeamshol
CRO: dšeor ctrrey kostei otrei ysteodain sorary dain dain deamšol
```
```
EVA: shor chkeey qoteey qokeody qoteold qokeol so raiin otal ykecho
CRO: šor hstei kotrei kosteody kotreold kosteol so rain otral ysteho
```
```
EVA: dcheor shol qokeeol chor chol qokeeody dorean
CRO: dheor šol kosteol hor hol kosteody dorean
```
```
EVA: folshody chol daiin fchodycheol cphol qotees shey oreso alcfhy
CRO: folšody hol dain fhodyheol cpllol kotres šey oreso alcplry
```
```
EVA: soiin chol cphol shol shol qockhol chor chol sho keey cckhhy ykeeam
CRO: soin hol cpllol šol šol kocstrol hor hol šo kei ccstrhy ysteam
```
```
EVA: saiichor sheor qockhody odeor yksheey chol sheody sai cheol raiin
CRO: saihor šeor kocstrody odeor ystšei hol šeody sai heol rain
```
```
EVA: sheor qkeeody chol daiin ctheol olcheol cheky cheol cheockhy okeol
CRO: šeor kosteody hol dain ctrreol olheol hesty heol heocstry osteol
```
```
EVA: yaiin chekeey chol cholody chos olchor qokeol okeeol cheols al
CRO: yain hestei hol holody hos olhor kosteol osteol heols al
```
```
EVA: chol cheol cho chckheody otolchey
CRO: hol heol ho hcstreody otrolhey
```

```
CRO: ctrrdectrry šeocplly kotreody cstroor ar hor otrei dain kostomo
```
```
EVA: sor cheey dair ol cheol qoolkeey chol cheey qokeol chotols

```
```
EVA: ykeeol chol chey eeoseeos sheeo okeol ches okeor okeol dy
CRO: ysteol hol hey eoseos šeo osteol hes osteor osteol dy
```
```

```

```
```

```
CRO: yheosty šostesy kostei hosteol soraloaly heor ol hocstrar
```

```
CRO: soral ostor ol hoy ly araroy ostar heeal heosteol orey
```

```
CRO: dain hesty hory
```

## F101R


**Text:**

```
EVA: pcheol cheol ol shey qockhol shor yteol sheockhey qpol cheor sain olo o qkeey chopcheey checkhey cpheocthy ykchy cheey chekeey dal chsm
CRO: pheol heol ol šey kocstrol šor ytreol šeocstrey koplol heor sain olo o kostei hoplhei hecstrey cplleoctrry ysthy hei hestei dal hsm
```
```
EVA: dol chokeey chkey cthey okal chol kol okeey r or ol okolol olchey qokchor okey qokeol kor shey teol or aiin chol daiin
CRO: dol hostei hstey ctrrey ostal hol kol ostei r or ol ostolol olhey kosthor ostey kosteol kor šey teol or ain hol dain
```
```
EVA: etolctheol okeor r sheol qotol sheo dol shey okeey ctheea yteeoldy kchdol sheody or ol sheor qotoiir otol sheey ssheo tchey ol dar am
CRO: etrolctrreol osteor r šeol kotrol šeo dol šey ostei ctrrea ytreoldy khdol šeody or ol šeor kotroir otrol šei sšeo they ol dar am
```
```
EVA: ycheeo or sheeol daiin sheeol okeol ctheol shkeeo qockheol daiin shy csol okeeor ctody chkchol doteoda okeol daisin okeey okeey dairin
CRO: yheo or šeol dain šeol osteol ctrreol šsteo kocstreol dain šy csol osteor ctrody hsthol dotreoda osteol daisin ostei ostei dairin
```
```
EVA: daiin ctheol cheol okor or aiin cheol cho keeo dchey okol okeol dor chol chy r aiin oteol oraiin olchey oteeod sheol okeol chosaiin sheom
CRO: dain ctrreol heol ostor or ain heol ho keo dhey ostol osteol dor hol hy r ain otreol orain olhey otreod šeol osteol hosain šeom
```
```
EVA: okeeol sho shody sho shol okeeeol cheos sheokeey sheeor chchy chodaiin sheeckhey teeol scheol sar oeeor
CRO: osteol šo šody šo šol osteeol heos šeostei šeor hhy hodain šecstrey teol sheol sar oeor
```
```
EVA: cphoar oaiin ypcholy daiin otaiin otaiin yfolaiin fcheolain ypchey yphooshotey odariin sheoor sheor ckheey ykhey qokchey cholp cheol dy
CRO: cplloar oain yplholy dain otrain otrain yprolain fheolain yplhey yplhoošotrey odarin šeoor šeor cstrei ysthey kosthey holpl heol dy
```
```
EVA: olaiin oteol chor oteey chokchey kor daiin shok chol chol qoky daiinol s al ydar daiin or ory okeey daiin shea daiin okol chear
CRO: olain otreol hor otrei hosthey kor dain šost hol hol kosty dainol s al ydar dain or ory ostei dain šea dain ostol hear
```
```
EVA: daiin okeol qokcheol ykeor dar ol otechy ykeor dor aiin chls cheolokol shey qodar soiin choko qokeol daiin odar okchol cheor chety
CRO: dain osteol kostheol ysteor dar ol otrehy ysteor dor ain hls heolostol šey kodar soin hosto kosteol dain odar osthol heor hetry
```
```
EVA: kor aithy ol chssho olcheeol kalshey okeoly oiin aiioly
CRO: kor aitrhy ol hsšo olheol kalšey osteoly oin aioly
```

**Text:**

```
EVA: tolchor cheopor or ody cpheyr shee fol soiin otsheey otokcho pcholy chor or choror sydorarokoraiin orolodain
CRO: tolhor heoplor or ody cplleyr še fol soin otršei otrostho pholy hor or horor sydorarostorain orolodain
```
```
EVA: or aiin or o or omam chor s aiin okor cheeor sheeol qokolol qoor cheey qokeod oeeo r choy sokeeodychodaiin cthy okody dar
CRO: or ain or o or omam hor s ain ostor heor šeol kostolol koor hei kosteod oeo r hoy sosteodyhodain ctrry ostody dar
```
```
EVA: ycheor oeo dain cheokal ykhody cheeods oraiin qoeey ctheyeocthy dain chedo dydy
CRO: yheor oeo dain heostal ysthody heods orain koei ctrreyeoctrry dain hedo dydy
```
```
EVA: kshar lol keeol otal or ol aiin okeod ykeey dain olcheolopcheol cthey qekeoldy qocthor sheody qockheey odaiin sho ytolaiir sodaiin dy
CRO: kšar lol keol otral or ol ain osteod ystei dain olheoloplheol ctrrey koesteoldy koctrror šeody kocstrei odain šo ytrolair sodain dy
```
```
EVA: oaiin ol olor daiin okeey qok ykeol daiin qockhy daiin olchdar qokeol dol oraiin oldaiin keeol rch qokeeeor sydy cheor okeey chol do dar
CRO: oain ol olor dain ostei kost ysteol dain kocstry dain olhdar kosteol dol orain oldain keol rh kosteeor sydy heor ostei hol do dar
```
```
EVA: teeal sheol qokeor qkhol olchor chokey chor ctheey dasdaiin cheeody cheey keo cheol daiiin deeor cheedy
CRO: teal šeol kosteor kosthol olhor hostey hor ctrrei dasdain heody hei keo heol daiin deor hedi
```
```
EVA: daiin dair yteol chor qockhol daiin ckheey chey kchey dosiin okeey ckheo lcheody kcheol daiin eteeys ctheody ctheockhosho olchor
CRO: dain dair ytreol hor kocstrol dain cstrei hey khey dosin ostei cstreo lheody kheol dain etreis ctrreody ctrreocstrošo olhor
```
```
EVA: olaiin okeol cheo kol ches sheey qoor qokeody cheor okeyoiin cheey cthey ory ctheey qokeey shol ody cheol oralar shey qokarary
CRO: olain osteol heo kol hes šei koor kosteody heor osteyoin hei ctrrey ory ctrrei kostei šol ody heol oralar šey kostarary
```
```
EVA: sol chol choly okeey dal qol shckheol chol cthear keeycheeo ol chs oraiin qokeeey saiir qodaiin cheol qokeey daiin cheodam
CRO: sol hol holy ostei dal kol šcstreol hol ctrrear keiheo ol hs orain kostei sair kodain heol kostei dain heodam
```
```
EVA: teol cheol ekcheyor cheol cthol cholaiin chol qkos
CRO: teol heol estheyor heol ctrrol holain hol kostos
```

```
CRO: dheo koeor oeoisthy heos ol or ol osteor ain
```

```
EVA: ycheey s odeeeey okeeor cheol or oiin oeees okear chey keey saiin oteos
CRO: yhei s odeei osteor heol or oin oees ostear hey kei sain otreos
```
```

CRO: doin or oin heol soir hol šei kocstry ol keor osteody osteor hos
```

```
CRO: otreo ostey šey ostey aies orei
```

```
CRO: sol hol kooin kostal heol hey kolhei dain heody dy
```

```
```

```
```

```

```

```

```

```

```
```

CRO: ysain cstrey koor heol
```

## F104R


## F105V

## F116R


**Text:**

```
EVA: kchdpy shey qokain otalshedy qteey shear ain or llory shear amom

```

## F86V


**Text:**

```
EVA: opor os sheody pchedar odsheo qody cheepchdy lpchedy olkar shdar dchdorqopcher cher oseeedar odaiin pcheodar chdair orarorchy shar opchsey otedy chcphhy chedy sar shed odar sheey scheor al cheefar shetchy qoteol otor shar qoteshy doin ofor arar dl
```
